# Analyzer Specification

> Generated by spec-gen v1.0.0 on 2026-03-09 23:34
> Source files: src/core/analyzer/repository-mapper.ts, src/api/types.ts, src/core/analyzer/embedding-service.ts, src/core/analyzer/subgraph-extractor.ts, src/core/analyzer/architecture-writer.ts, src/core/analyzer/dependency-graph.ts, src/core/analyzer/spec-vector-index.ts, src/core/analyzer/file-walker.ts, src/core/analyzer/refactor-analyzer.ts, src/core/analyzer/vector-index.ts, src/core/analyzer/import-parser.ts, src/core/analyzer/signature-extractor.ts, src/core/analyzer/artifact-generator.ts, src/core/analyzer/call-graph.ts, src/core/analyzer/duplicate-detector.ts, src/core/analyzer/significance-scorer.ts

## Purpose

[PARTIAL SPEC — file too large to fully analyze (2 parts)] Analyzes call graphs and requirement
mappings to identify refactoring priorities and issues in codebase.

## Entities

### LanguageBreakdown

Represents the distribution of programming languages in the repository.

**Properties:**

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| languages | Array<{name: string, percentage: number}> | List of languages and their percentages |

### DetectedFramework

Represents a detected framework in the repository.

**Properties:**

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| name | string | Name of the framework |
| version | string | Version of the framework |

### DirectoryStats

Represents statistics for a directory in the repository.

**Properties:**

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| path | string | Path to the directory |
| fileCount | number | Number of files in the directory |
| lineCount | number | Total lines of code in the directory |

### FileClusters

Represents clusters of files by domain/layer in the repository.

**Properties:**

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| clusters | Array<{domain: string, layer: string, files: Array<string>}> | List of file clusters |

### RepositoryMapMetadata

Represents metadata for a repository map.

**Properties:**

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| projectName | string | Name of the project |
| projectType | string | Type of the project |
| generatedAt | Date | Date when the map was generated |

### RepositoryMapSummary

Represents a summary of a repository map.

**Properties:**

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| totalFiles | number | Total number of files in the repository |
| totalLines | number | Total lines of code in the repository |
| languageBreakdown | LanguageBreakdown | Language breakdown in the repository |
| detectedFrameworks | Array<DetectedFramework> | List of detected frameworks |

### RepositoryMap

Represents a complete map of the repository.

**Properties:**

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| metadata | RepositoryMapMetadata | Metadata for the repository map |
| summary | RepositoryMapSummary | Summary of the repository map |
| directoryStats | Array<DirectoryStats> | Directory statistics for the repository |
| fileClusters | FileClusters | File clusters by domain/layer |

### RepositoryMapperOptions

Represents options for repository mapping.

**Properties:**

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| outputDir | string | Output directory for the repository map |
| ignorePatterns | Array<string> | Patterns to ignore during mapping |

### RepositoryMapper

Represents a mapper for generating a repository map.

**Properties:**

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| rootPath | string | Root path of the repository |
| options | RepositoryMapperOptions | Options for repository mapping |

### AnalyzeResult

Result of analyzing the project codebase.

**Properties:**

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| repoMap | CoreRepositoryMap | Repository map of the analyzed codebase |
| depGraph | DependencyGraphResult | Dependency graph of the analyzed codebase |
| artifacts | AnalysisArtifacts | Analysis artifacts generated |
| duration | number | Duration of the analysis in milliseconds |

### EmbeddingConfig

Configuration for the EmbeddingService, specifying the API endpoint, model, and optional parameters.

**Properties:**

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| baseUrl | string | Base URL of the OpenAI-compatible API |
| model | string | Embedding model name |
| apiKey | string | API key for authentication |
| batchSize | number | Maximum number of texts per API call |
| skipSslVerify | boolean | Disable SSL certificate verification |

### EmbeddingService

Service for computing text embeddings via any OpenAI-compatible `/embeddings` endpoint.

**Properties:**

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| baseUrl | string | Base URL of the OpenAI-compatible API |
| model | string | Embedding model name |
| apiKey | string | API key for authentication |
| batchSize | number | Maximum number of texts per API call |

**Relationships:**

- uses EmbeddingConfig (EmbeddingService uses EmbeddingConfig for configuration)

### SubGraphNode

Represents a node in a subgraph, typically a function with its call relationships.

**Properties:**

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| name | string | Name of the function |
| file | string | File path where the function is defined |
| fanIn | number | Number of incoming calls to the function |
| fanOut | number | Number of outgoing calls from the function |

### SubGraph

Represents a subgraph of function calls, typically centered around a 'god function'.

**Properties:**

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| root | SubGraphNode | The root node of the subgraph |
| nodes | SubGraphNode[] | Nodes reachable within MAX_DEPTH |
| edges | Array<[string, string]> | Caller-callee pairs |

### FunctionNode

Represents a function node in the call graph.

**Properties:**

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| id | string | Unique identifier for the function |
| name | string | Name of the function |
| filePath | string | File path where the function is defined |
| fanIn | number | Number of incoming calls to the function |
| fanOut | number | Number of outgoing calls from the function |

### SerializedCallGraph

Represents a serialized call graph with nodes and edges.

**Properties:**

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| nodes | FunctionNode[] | List of function nodes |
| edges | Array<{callerId: string, calleeId: string}> | List of caller-callee edges |

### FileSignatureMap

Represents a map of file signatures, typically used for documentation purposes.

**Properties:**

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| path | string | File path |
| entries | Array<{signature: string, docstring: string}> | List of function signatures and their docstrings |

### ClusterSummary

[PARTIAL SPEC — file too large to fully analyze (2 parts)] Represents a summary of a module cluster
in the architecture.

**Properties:**

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| id | string | Unique identifier for the cluster |
| name | string | Name of the cluster |
| fileCount | number | Number of files in the cluster |
| role | string | Architectural role of the cluster |
| entryPointCount | number | Number of entry points in the cluster |
| hubCount | number | Number of hubs in the cluster |
| dependsOn | string[] | List of cluster IDs this cluster depends on |
| keyFiles | string[] | List of key files in the cluster |

### ArchitectureOverview

[PARTIAL SPEC — file too large to fully analyze (2 parts)] Represents a high-level overview of the
architecture.

**Properties:**

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| generatedAt | string | Timestamp when the overview was generated |
| summary | object | Summary statistics of the architecture |
| clusters | ClusterSummary[] | List of module clusters |
| globalEntryPoints | object[] | List of global entry points |
| criticalHubs | object[] | List of critical hubs |

**Relationships:**

- has-many ClusterSummary (ArchitectureOverview contains many ClusterSummary objects)

### Component

[PARTIAL SPEC — file too large to fully analyze (2 parts)] Represents a key component in the
architecture.

**Properties:**

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| name | string | Name of the component |
| role | string | Role of the component |
| keyFiles | Array<string> | List of key files in the component |

### EntryPoint

[PARTIAL SPEC — file too large to fully analyze (2 parts)] Represents an entry point in the codebase
with no internal callers.

**Properties:**

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| name | string | Name of the entry point |
| file | string | File containing the entry point |
| language | string | Programming language of the entry point |

### CriticalHub

[PARTIAL SPEC — file too large to fully analyze (2 parts)] Represents a high fan-in function in the
codebase.

**Properties:**

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| name | string | Name of the critical hub |
| file | string | File containing the critical hub |
| fanIn | number | Number of callers to the function |
| fanOut | number | Number of functions called by the function |

### DependencyNode

Represents a node in the dependency graph, typically corresponding to a file or module.

**Properties:**

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| id | string | Unique identifier for the node |
| name | string | Name of the file or module |
| type | string | Type of the node (e.g., file, module) |
| degree | number | Number of connections to other nodes |
| betweenness | number | Betweenness centrality measure |
| pageRank | number | PageRank measure |
| clusterId | string | Identifier for the cluster the node belongs to |
| imports | string[] | List of imports from other nodes |
| exports | string[] | List of exports to other nodes |

**Relationships:**

- has-many DependencyEdge (A node can have many edges connecting it to other nodes)
- belongs to FileCluster (A node belongs to a file cluster)

### DependencyEdge

Represents an edge in the dependency graph, connecting two nodes.

**Properties:**

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| source | string | Source node ID |
| target | string | Target node ID |
| type | string | Type of the edge (e.g., import, export) |
| weight | number | Weight of the edge |

**Relationships:**

- belongs to DependencyNode (An edge connects two nodes)

### FileCluster

Represents a cluster of related files or modules in the dependency graph.

**Properties:**

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| id | string | Unique identifier for the cluster |
| name | string | Name of the cluster |
| nodes | DependencyNode[] | List of nodes in the cluster |
| domainName | string | Suggested domain name for the cluster |

**Relationships:**

- has-many DependencyNode (A cluster can contain many nodes)

### DependencyGraphResult

Represents the complete dependency graph result, including nodes, edges, clusters, and statistics.

**Properties:**

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| nodes | DependencyNode[] | List of nodes in the graph |
| edges | DependencyEdge[] | List of edges in the graph |
| clusters | FileCluster[] | List of clusters in the graph |
| cycles | string[][] | List of cycles detected in the graph |
| statistics | object | Statistics about the graph |

**Relationships:**

- has-many DependencyNode (Graph result contains many nodes)
- has-many DependencyEdge (Graph result contains many edges)
- has-many FileCluster (Graph result contains many clusters)

### DependencyGraphOptions

Represents options for building the dependency graph.

**Properties:**

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| maxNodes | number | Maximum number of nodes to include in the graph |
| maxEdges | number | Maximum number of edges to include in the graph |
| includeExternal | boolean | Whether to include external dependencies |
| includeTests | boolean | Whether to include test files |

### DependencyGraphBuilder

Builds and analyzes a dependency graph from scored files.

**Relationships:**

- uses DependencyGraphOptions (Builder uses options to configure the graph building process)
- produces DependencyGraphResult (Builder produces a dependency graph result)

### SpecRecord

[PARTIAL SPEC — file too large to fully analyze (2 parts)] Represents a logical section from a
Markdown spec file, used for vector indexing.

**Properties:**

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| id | string | Unique identifier combining domain and section |
| domain | string | Domain or category of the specification |
| section | string | Type of section (requirements, purpose, entities, etc.) |
| title | string | Title of the section |
| text | string | Concatenated text used for embedding |
| linkedFiles | string | JSON-encoded string array of source files linked to this section |
| vector | number[] | Embedding vector for the section |

### SpecSearchResult

[PARTIAL SPEC — file too large to fully analyze (2 parts)] Represents a search result from querying
the SpecVectorIndex.

**Properties:**

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| record | object | The matching SpecRecord |
| score | number | Relevance score of the match |

**Relationships:**

- contains SpecRecord (SpecSearchResult contains a SpecRecord)

### MappingEntry

[PARTIAL SPEC — file too large to fully analyze (2 parts)] Represents a mapping entry from
mapping.json, linking requirements to source files.

**Properties:**

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| requirement | string | Name of the requirement |
| service | string | Service associated with the requirement |
| domain | string | Domain or category of the requirement |
| specFile | string | Path to the specification file |
| functions | array | Array of function objects linked to the requirement |

**Properties:**

| Name | Type | Description |

| section | string | Type of section (requirements, purpose, entities, etc.) |
| title | string | Title of the section |
| content | string | Content of the section |
| requirementKey | string | Slugified requirement name for mapping lookup |

### SpecFile

[PARTIAL SPEC — file too large to fully analyze (2 parts)] Represents a specification file
containing requirements and sections.

**Properties:**

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| path | string | File system path to the specification file |
| domain | string | Domain or category the specification belongs to |

**Relationships:**

- has-many SpecSection (A specification file contains multiple sections)

### SpecSection

[PARTIAL SPEC — file too large to fully analyze (2 parts)] A section within a specification file
containing a requirement or information.

**Properties:**

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| section | string | Section identifier |
| title | string | Title of the section |
| requirementKey | string | Key for the requirement if this section represents one |
| text | string | Content of the section |

**Relationships:**

- belongs to SpecFile (Section belongs to a specification file)

### FileMetadata

[PARTIAL SPEC — file too large to fully analyze (2 parts)] Metadata about a file in the codebase,
including its significance and properties for analysis.

**Properties:**

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| path | string | Absolute path to the file |
| relativePath | string | Path relative to the root directory |
| name | string | Name of the file |
| extension | string | File extension |
| size | number | Size of the file in bytes |
| lines | number | Number of lines in the file |
| isTest | boolean | Whether the file is a test file |
| isConfig | boolean | Whether the file is a configuration file |
| isGenerated | boolean | Whether the file is likely generated |
| isEntryPoint | boolean | Whether the file is likely an entry point |
| hasShebang | boolean | Whether the file has a shebang line |
| significance | number | Significance score of the file |

### FileWalkerResult

[PARTIAL SPEC — file too large to fully analyze (2 parts)] Result of the file walking process,
including collected files and statistics.

**Properties:**

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| files | FileMetadata[] | Array of collected file metadata |
| skippedCount | number | Number of files skipped |
| skippedReasons | Record<string, number> | Reasons for skipping files and their counts |
| directoriesScanned | number | Number of directories scanned |
| extensionCounts | Record<string, number> | Counts of files by extension |
| directoryCounts | Record<string, number> | Counts of files by directory |

### FileWalkerOptions

[PARTIAL SPEC — file too large to fully analyze (2 parts)] Options for configuring the FileWalker
behavior.

**Properties:**

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| maxFiles | number | Maximum number of files to process |
| includePatterns | string[] | Additional glob patterns to include |
| excludePatterns | string[] | Additional glob patterns to exclude |
| onProgress | function | Progress callback for UI updates |
| signal | AbortSignal | AbortController signal for cancellation |
| concurrency | number | Maximum concurrent file reads |

### FileWalkerProgress

[PARTIAL SPEC — file too large to fully analyze (2 parts)] Progress information during file walking.

**Properties:**

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| filesFound | number | Number of files found |
| directoriesScanned | number | Number of directories scanned |
| currentPath | string | Current path being processed |

### FileWalker

[PARTIAL SPEC — file too large to fully analyze (2 parts)] A utility for traversing directories and
collecting metadata about files.

**Properties:**

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| options | FileWalkerOptions | Configuration options for the file walker. |
| rootPath | string | The root directory path to start walking from. |
| files | FileMetadata[] | Array of metadata for files found during the walk. |
| directoriesScanned | number | Count of directories scanned during the walk. |
| skippedCount | number | Count of files and directories skipped during the walk. |
| skippedReasons | Record<string, number> | Reasons for skipping files and directories, with counts. |
| extensionCounts | Record<string, number> | Counts of files by their extensions. |
| directoryCounts | Record<string, number> | Counts of files by their directories. |
| ig | Ignore | Instance for handling ignore patterns. |
| igInclude | Ignore | Instance for handling include patterns. |

**Relationships:**

- has-many FileMetadata (FileWalker collects metadata for multiple files.)
- has-one FileWalkerOptions (FileWalker uses configuration options.)

### RefactorEntry

[PARTIAL SPEC — file too large to fully analyze (2 parts)] Represents a function with refactoring
issues and priority score.

**Properties:**

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| function | string | Function name |
| file | string | File path |
| className | string | Class name if applicable |
| fanIn | number | Number of internal callers |
| fanOut | number | Number of internal callees |
| depth | number | Hops from nearest entry point (-1 = unreachable) |
| sccSize | number | Strongly connected component size (>1 = in a cycle) |
| requirements | string[] | List of requirement names this function implements |
| issues | RefactorIssue[] | List of refactoring issues |
| priorityScore | number | Composite priority score for sorting (higher = more urgent) |

### CycleSummary

[PARTIAL SPEC — file too large to fully analyze (2 parts)] Summary of a cyclic dependency in the
codebase.

**Properties:**

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| sccId | number | Unique identifier for the strongly connected component |
| size | number | Number of functions in the cycle |
| participants | Array<{function: string; file: string}> | List of functions and their file paths involved in the cycle |

### RefactorReport

[PARTIAL SPEC — file too large to fully analyze (2 parts)] Report of refactoring priorities and
issues detected in the codebase.

**Properties:**

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| generatedAt | string | Timestamp when the report was generated |
| stats | object | Statistics about the refactoring analysis |
| priorities | RefactorEntry[] | Functions with at least one issue, sorted by priorityScore descending |
| cycles | CycleSummary[] | List of cyclic dependencies detected |

### FunctionRecord

Represents a function in the codebase with its metadata and embedding vector.

**Properties:**

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| id | string | Unique identifier for the function |
| name | string | Name of the function |
| filePath | string | Path to the file containing the function |
| className | string | Name of the class containing the function, if applicable |
| language | string | Programming language of the function |
| signature | string | Function signature |
| docstring | string | Documentation string for the function |
| fanIn | number | Number of incoming calls to the function |
| fanOut | number | Number of outgoing calls from the function |
| isHub | boolean | Indicates if the function is a hub in the call graph |
| isEntryPoint | boolean | Indicates if the function is an entry point in the call graph |
| text | string | Concatenated text used for embedding |
| vector | number[] | Embedding vector for the function |

### SearchResult

Represents the result of a semantic search query.

**Properties:**

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| record | Omit<FunctionRecord, 'vector'> | Function record without the vector |
| score | number | Distance score (lower = more similar) |

### VectorIndex

Builds and queries a LanceDB vector index over the call graph functions.

**Relationships:**

- uses FunctionNode (Uses FunctionNode data to build the index)
- uses FileSignatureMap (Uses FileSignatureMap data to enrich function records)
- uses EmbeddingService (Uses EmbeddingService to generate embeddings)

### ImportInfo

[PARTIAL SPEC — file too large to fully analyze (4 parts)] Information about an import statement in
a source file.

**Properties:**

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| source | string | The source path of the import |
| isRelative | boolean | Whether the import is relative |
| isPackage | boolean | Whether the import is from a package |
| isBuiltin | boolean | Whether the import is a Node.js builtin |
| importedNames | string[] | Names of the imported items |
| hasDefault | boolean | Whether the import has a default import |
| hasNamespace | boolean | Whether the import has a namespace import |
| isTypeOnly | boolean | Whether the import is type-only |
| isDynamic | boolean | Whether the import is dynamic |
| line | number | Line number where the import occurs |

### ExportInfo

[PARTIAL SPEC — file too large to fully analyze (4 parts)] Information about an export statement in
a source file.

**Properties:**

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| name | string | Name of the exported item |
| isDefault | boolean | Whether the export is default |
| isType | boolean | Whether the export is a type |
| isReExport | boolean | Whether the export is a re-export |
| reExportSource | string | Source of the re-export |
| kind | 'function' | 'class' | 'variable' | 'type' | 'interface' | 'enum' | 'unknown' | Kind of the exported item |
| line | number | Line number where the export occurs |

### FileAnalysis

[PARTIAL SPEC — file too large to fully analyze (4 parts)] Complete analysis of a file's imports and
exports.

**Properties:**

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| filePath | string | Path to the analyzed file |
| imports | ImportInfo[] | List of imports in the file |
| exports | ExportInfo[] | List of exports in the file |
| localImports | string[] | List of local imports |
| externalImports | string[] | List of external imports |
| parseErrors | string[] | List of parsing errors |

**Relationships:**

- contains ImportInfo (FileAnalysis contains multiple ImportInfo objects)
- contains ExportInfo (FileAnalysis contains multiple ExportInfo objects)

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| baseDir | string | Base directory for resolving relative imports |

| extensions | string[] | File extensions to try when resolving |

[PARTIAL SPEC — file too large to fully analyze (4 parts)] Represents an import statement in
JavaScript/TypeScript code.

**Properties:**

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| source | string | The source module being imported |
| isRelative | boolean | Whether the import is relative |
| isPackage | boolean | Whether the import is from a package |
| isBuiltin | boolean | Whether the import is from a built-in module |
| importedNames | string[] | Names being imported |
| hasDefault | boolean | Whether a default import exists |
| hasNamespace | boolean | Whether a namespace import exists |
| isTypeOnly | boolean | Whether the import is type-only |
| isDynamic | boolean | Whether the import is dynamic |
| line | number | Line number where the import occurs |

[PARTIAL SPEC — file too large to fully analyze (4 parts)] Represents an export statement in
JavaScript/TypeScript code.

**Properties:**

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| name | string | Name of the exported entity |
| isDefault | boolean | Whether the export is default |
| isType | boolean | Whether the export is a type |
| isReExport | boolean | Whether the export is a re-export |
| reExportSource | string | Source module for re-exports |
| kind | string | Kind of export (class, function, variable, etc.) |
| line | number | Line number where the export occurs |

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| cache | Map<string, FileAnalysis> | Cache for storing parsed file analyses |

### ExtractedSignature

[PARTIAL SPEC — file too large to fully analyze (3 parts)] Represents a function, class, method,
interface, or type signature extracted from source code.

**Properties:**

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| kind | string | The type of signature (class, function, method, interface, type) |
| name | string | The name of the signature |
| signature | string | A compact one-liner representation of the signature |
| docstring | string | The first meaningful line of the doc comment |
| decorator | string | Decorator applied to the signature (e.g., @router.get('/path') for FastAPI) |

Options for artifact generation.

LLM context phase.

All generated artifacts.

Detected domain (maps to OpenSpec spec).

Architecture node information for simplified view.

### CallEdge

Represents a call relationship between two functions in the call graph.

**Properties:**

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| source | string | ID of the source function |
| target | string | ID of the target function |

**Relationships:**

- belongs to FunctionNode (CallEdge connects two FunctionNodes)

### LayerViolation

Represents a violation of layer architecture rules in the call graph.

**Properties:**

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| source | string | ID of the source function |
| target | string | ID of the target function |
| sourceLayer | string | Layer of the source function |
| targetLayer | string | Layer of the target function |

**Relationships:**

- belongs to FunctionNode (LayerViolation involves two FunctionNodes)

### CallGraphResult

Represents the result of call graph analysis.

**Properties:**

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| nodes | FunctionNode[] | Array of function nodes in the call graph |
| edges | CallEdge[] | Array of call edges in the call graph |
| violations | LayerViolation[] | Array of layer violations in the call graph |

**Relationships:**

- has-many FunctionNode (CallGraphResult contains many FunctionNodes)
- has-many CallEdge (CallGraphResult contains many CallEdges)
- has-many LayerViolation (CallGraphResult contains many LayerViolations)

### CallGraphBuilder

Class responsible for building the call graph.

### serializeCallGraph

Function to serialize a CallGraphResult into a SerializedCallGraph.

**Relationships:**

- converts CallGraphResult (serializeCallGraph converts CallGraphResult to SerializedCallGraph)

### CloneInstance

Represents a specific instance of a code clone.

**Properties:**

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| filePath | string | Path to the file containing the clone |
| startLine | number | Starting line number of the clone |
| endLine | number | Ending line number of the clone |
| content | string | Content of the clone |

**Relationships:**

- belongs to CloneGroup (Clone instance belongs to a clone group)

### CloneType

Represents the type of a code clone.

### CloneGroup

Represents a group of code clones that are similar to each other.

**Properties:**

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| instances | CloneInstance[] | Array of clone instances in the group |
| type | CloneType | Type of the clone group |
| similarity | number | Similarity score of the clone group |

### DuplicateDetectionResult

Represents the result of a duplicate detection operation.

**Properties:**

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| cloneGroups | CloneGroup[] | Array of clone groups found |
| totalFiles | number | Total number of files analyzed |
| totalLines | number | Total number of lines analyzed |

### ScoringConfig

[PARTIAL SPEC — file too large to fully analyze (2 parts)] Configuration for custom scoring rules in
the file significance scorer.

**Properties:**

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| highValueNames | Record<string, number> | Custom high-value name patterns with scores |
| negativeNames | Record<string, number> | Custom negative name patterns with scores |
| highValuePaths | Record<string, number> | Custom high-value path patterns with scores |
| minScore | number | Minimum score to include in results |

### FileRelationship

[PARTIAL SPEC — file too large to fully analyze (2 parts)] Import/export relationship for
connectivity scoring.

**Properties:**

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| filePath | string | Path to the file |
| imports | string[] | List of files imported by this file |
| importedBy | string[] | List of files that import this file |

### ScoredFile

[PARTIAL SPEC — file too large to fully analyze (2 parts)] Represents a file with its significance
score and tags.

**Properties:**

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| score | number | Total significance score of the file |
| scoreBreakdown | object | Breakdown of the score by different factors |
| tags | string[] | Tags associated with the file |

**Relationships:**

- extends FileMetadata (Inherits properties from FileMetadata)

### SignificanceScorer

[PARTIAL SPEC — file too large to fully analyze (2 parts)] Class responsible for scoring files based
on various factors.

**Properties:**

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| config | ScoringConfig | Configuration for scoring |
| relationships | Map<string, FileRelationship> | Map of file relationships |

## Requirements

### Requirement: EmbeddingConfigValidation

The system SHALL validate EmbeddingConfig according to these rules:
- baseUrl must be a valid URL
- model must be a non-empty string
- batchSize must be a positive integer if provided

#### Scenario: CreateEmbeddingconfig
- **GIVEN** Valid configuration parameters
- **WHEN** EmbeddingConfig is instantiated
- **THEN** EmbeddingConfig object is created with the provided parameters

### Requirement: EmbeddingServiceValidation

The system SHALL validate EmbeddingService according to these rules:
- baseUrl must be a valid URL
- model must be a non-empty string
- batchSize must be a positive integer if provided
- texts must be a non-empty array of strings

#### Scenario: CreateEmbeddingserviceFromEnvironmentVariables
- **GIVEN** Environment variables EMBED_BASE_URL and EMBED_MODEL are set
- **WHEN** EmbeddingService.fromEnv() is called
- **THEN** EmbeddingService object is created with the provided environment variables

#### Scenario: CreateEmbeddingserviceFromSpecgenconfig
- **GIVEN** SpecGenConfig with embedding configuration
- **WHEN** EmbeddingService.fromConfig() is called
- **THEN** EmbeddingService object is created with the provided configuration

#### Scenario: ComputeEmbeddingsForAListOfTexts
- **GIVEN** A list of texts
- **WHEN** embed() is called
- **THEN** Embeddings are computed for each text and returned in the same order

### Requirement: DependencyNodeValidation

The system SHALL validate DependencyNode according to these rules:
- Node must have a unique id
- Node must have a name
- Node must have a type

#### Scenario: CreateDependencynode
- **GIVEN** A file or module with imports and exports
- **WHEN** DependencyNode is created
- **THEN** Node is initialized with id, name, type, and lists of imports and exports

### Requirement: DependencyEdgeValidation

The system SHALL validate DependencyEdge according to these rules:
- Edge must have a source node ID
- Edge must have a target node ID
- Edge must have a type

#### Scenario: CreateDependencyedge
- **GIVEN** Two nodes with a dependency relationship
- **WHEN** DependencyEdge is created
- **THEN** Edge is initialized with source, target, and type

### Requirement: FileClusterValidation

The system SHALL validate FileCluster according to these rules:
- Cluster must have a unique id
- Cluster must have a name
- Cluster must contain at least one node

#### Scenario: CreateFilecluster
- **GIVEN** A group of related nodes
- **WHEN** FileCluster is created
- **THEN** Cluster is initialized with id, name, and list of nodes

### Requirement: DependencyGraphResultValidation

The system SHALL validate DependencyGraphResult according to these rules:
- Graph result must contain at least one node
- Graph result must contain at least one edge

#### Scenario: CreateDependencygraphresult
- **GIVEN** A built dependency graph with nodes, edges, clusters, cycles, and statistics
- **WHEN** DependencyGraphResult is created
- **THEN** Graph result is initialized with nodes, edges, clusters, cycles, and statistics

### Requirement: SpecRecordValidation

The system SHALL validate SpecRecord according to these rules:
- id must be unique
- section must be one of: requirements, purpose, entities, design, architecture, other
- linkedFiles must be a valid JSON-encoded string array

#### Scenario: CreateSpecrecord
- **GIVEN** A parsed section from a Markdown file
- **WHEN** buildText() is called
- **THEN** A SpecRecord is created with the section's text and metadata

### Requirement: SpecSearchResultValidation

The system SHALL validate SpecSearchResult according to these rules:
- score must be a number between 0 and 1

#### Scenario: SearchSpecvectorindex
- **GIVEN** A built SpecVectorIndex
- **WHEN** search() is called with a query
- **THEN** An array of SpecSearchResults is returned, sorted by relevance

### Requirement: MappingEntryValidation

The system SHALL validate MappingEntry according to these rules:
- requirement must be a non-empty string
- domain must be a non-empty string
- functions must be an array of objects with name and file properties

#### Scenario: ValidMappingEntryAccepted
- **GIVEN** A valid MappingEntry object with all required fields
- **WHEN** The object is validated
- **THEN** Validation passes with no errors

### Requirement: ParsedSectionValidation

The system SHALL validate ParsedSection according to these rules:
- section must be one of: requirements, purpose, entities, design, architecture, other
- title must be a non-empty string
- content must be a non-empty string

#### Scenario: ParseMarkdownFile
- **GIVEN** A Markdown file
- **WHEN** parseSpecFile() is called
- **THEN** An array of ParsedSection objects is returned

### Requirement: SpecFileValidation

The system SHALL validate SpecFile according to these rules:
- File must exist and be readable
- File must be in markdown format

#### Scenario: ParseSpecificationFile
- **GIVEN** Valid specification file path
- **WHEN** parseSpecFile() is called
- **THEN** Returns array of SpecSection objects

### Requirement: SpecSectionValidation

The system SHALL validate SpecSection according to these rules:
- Section must have a unique identifier
- Text content must not be empty

#### Scenario: BuildSectionText
- **GIVEN** Valid SpecSection object
- **WHEN** buildText() is called
- **THEN** Returns formatted text content for the section

### Requirement: FileWalkerValidation

The system SHALL validate FileWalker according to these rules:
- maxFiles must be a positive integer
- concurrency must be a positive integer
- includePatterns and excludePatterns must be arrays of strings

#### Scenario: WalkDirectory
- **GIVEN** A root directory path and optional options
- **WHEN** walk() is called
- **THEN** FileWalker traverses the directory, collects file metadata, and returns a result with files and
summary.

#### Scenario: SkipDirectory
- **GIVEN** A directory name and depth
- **WHEN** shouldSkipDirectory() is called
- **THEN** Returns true if the directory should be skipped based on patterns or predefined rules.

#### Scenario: SkipFile
- **GIVEN** A file path
- **WHEN** shouldSkipFile() is called
- **THEN** Returns true if the file should be skipped based on patterns or predefined rules.

#### Scenario: ProcessFile
- **GIVEN** A file path and metadata
- **WHEN** processFile() is called
- **THEN** Collects metadata for the file and updates counts.

### Requirement: VectorIndexValidation

The system SHALL validate VectorIndex according to these rules:
- Nodes array must not be empty when building the index
- Number of generated embeddings must match the number of function records
- Vector index must exist before performing a search

#### Scenario: BuildVectorIndex
- **GIVEN** A set of function nodes, signatures, hub IDs, entry point IDs, and an embedding service
- **WHEN** VectorIndex.build() is called
- **THEN** A LanceDB vector index is created with function records including embeddings

#### Scenario: SearchVectorIndex
- **GIVEN** An existing vector index and an embedding service
- **WHEN** VectorIndex.search() is called with a query
- **THEN** A list of search results is returned, sorted by similarity to the query

#### Scenario: CheckIndexExistence
- **GIVEN** An output directory
- **WHEN** VectorIndex.exists() is called
- **THEN** Returns true if a vector index exists in the specified directory, false otherwise

### Requirement: ImportInfoValidation

The system SHALL validate ImportInfo according to these rules:
- source must be a non-empty string
- line must be a positive integer

#### Scenario: ParseDefaultImport
- **GIVEN** Content with 'import X from "module"'
- **WHEN** parseJSImports() is called
- **THEN** ImportInfo with hasDefault=true and importedNames=[X] is created

#### Scenario: ParseNamedImport
- **GIVEN** Content with 'import {X, Y} from "module"'
- **WHEN** parseJSImports() is called
- **THEN** ImportInfo with hasDefault=false and importedNames=[X, Y] is created

### Requirement: ExportInfoValidation

The system SHALL validate ExportInfo according to these rules:
- name must be a non-empty string
- line must be a positive integer
- kind must be one of the specified values

#### Scenario: ValidExportInfoAccepted
- **GIVEN** A valid ExportInfo object with all required fields
- **WHEN** The object is validated
- **THEN** Validation passes with no errors

### Requirement: FileAnalysisValidation

The system SHALL validate FileAnalysis according to these rules:
- filePath must be a non-empty string
- imports must be an array of ImportInfo objects
- exports must be an array of ExportInfo objects

#### Scenario: ValidFileAnalysisAccepted
- **GIVEN** A valid FileAnalysis object with all required fields
- **WHEN** The object is validated
- **THEN** Validation passes with no errors

### Requirement: ResolveOptionsValidation

The system SHALL validate ResolveOptions according to these rules:
- baseDir must be a non-empty string
- pathAliases must be an object with string keys and string array values
- extensions must be an array of strings

#### Scenario: ValidResolveOptionsAccepted
- **GIVEN** A valid ResolveOptions object with all required fields
- **WHEN** The object is validated
- **THEN** Validation passes with no errors

### Requirement: ImportValidation

The system SHALL validate Import according to these rules:
- Source must be a non-empty string
- At least one of isRelative, isPackage, or isBuiltin must be true
- If hasDefault is true, importedNames must be empty or contain only one name

#### Scenario: ParseEs6Import
- **GIVEN** JavaScript/TypeScript content with ES6 import statement
- **WHEN** parseJSImports() is called
- **THEN** Import object created with correct properties for ES6 import

#### Scenario: ParseTypeOnlyImport
- **GIVEN** JavaScript/TypeScript content with type-only import statement
- **WHEN** parseJSImports() is called
- **THEN** Import object created with isTypeOnly set to true

#### Scenario: ParseCommonjsRequire
- **GIVEN** JavaScript/TypeScript content with CommonJS require statement
- **WHEN** parseJSImports() is called
- **THEN** Import object created with correct properties for CommonJS require

#### Scenario: ParseDynamicImport
- **GIVEN** JavaScript/TypeScript content with dynamic import statement
- **WHEN** parseJSImports() is called
- **THEN** Import object created with isDynamic set to true

### Requirement: ExportValidation

The system SHALL validate Export according to these rules:
- Name must be a non-empty string
- Kind must be one of: 'class', 'function', 'variable', 'type', 'interface', 'enum', 'unknown'
- If isReExport is true, reExportSource must be a non-empty string

#### Scenario: ParseDefaultExport
- **GIVEN** JavaScript/TypeScript content with default export statement
- **WHEN** parseJSExports() is called
- **THEN** Export object created with isDefault set to true

#### Scenario: ParseNamedExport
- **GIVEN** JavaScript/TypeScript content with named export statement
- **WHEN** parseJSExports() is called
- **THEN** Export objects created for each named export

#### Scenario: ParseVariableExport
- **GIVEN** JavaScript/TypeScript content with variable export statement
- **WHEN** parseJSExports() is called
- **THEN** Export object created with kind set to 'variable'

#### Scenario: ParseFunctionExport
- **GIVEN** JavaScript/TypeScript content with function export statement
- **WHEN** parseJSExports() is called
- **THEN** Export object created with kind set to 'function'

#### Scenario: ParseClassExport
- **GIVEN** JavaScript/TypeScript content with class export statement
- **WHEN** parseJSExports() is called
- **THEN** Export object created with kind set to 'class'

#### Scenario: ParseTypeExport
- **GIVEN** JavaScript/TypeScript content with type export statement
- **WHEN** parseJSExports() is called
- **THEN** Export object created with isType set to true and kind set to 'type'

#### Scenario: ParseInterfaceExport
- **GIVEN** JavaScript/TypeScript content with interface export statement
- **WHEN** parseJSExports() is called
- **THEN** Export object created with isType set to true and kind set to 'interface'

#### Scenario: ParseEnumExport
- **GIVEN** JavaScript/TypeScript content with enum export statement
- **WHEN** parseJSExports() is called
- **THEN** Export object created with kind set to 'enum'

#### Scenario: ParseReExportAll
- **GIVEN** JavaScript/TypeScript content with re-export all statement
- **WHEN** parseJSExports() is called
- **THEN** Export object created with isReExport set to true and reExportSource set to the source module

#### Scenario: ParseCommonjsModule.exports
- **GIVEN** JavaScript/TypeScript content with CommonJS module.exports statement
- **WHEN** parseJSExports() is called
- **THEN** Export object created with isDefault set to true

#### Scenario: ParseCommonjsExports.x
- **GIVEN** JavaScript/TypeScript content with CommonJS exports.X statement
- **WHEN** parseJSExports() is called
- **THEN** Export object created with name set to X

### Requirement: ImportExportParserValidation

The system SHALL validate ImportExportParser according to these rules:
- File type must be supported (js, ts, python)
- Cache is cleared when clearCache() is called

#### Scenario: ParseSingleFile
- **GIVEN** A valid file path
- **WHEN** parseFile() is called
- **THEN** FileAnalysis is returned with imports, exports, and categorized imports

#### Scenario: ParseMultipleFiles
- **GIVEN** An array of valid file paths
- **WHEN** parseFiles() is called
- **THEN** Map of file paths to FileAnalysis instances is returned

#### Scenario: CacheHit
- **GIVEN** A file path that has been previously parsed
- **WHEN** parseFile() is called
- **THEN** Cached FileAnalysis is returned without re-parsing

### Requirement: CloneInstanceValidation

The system SHALL validate CloneInstance according to these rules:
- startLine must be less than or equal to endLine

#### Scenario: ValidCloneInstanceAccepted
- **GIVEN** A valid CloneInstance object with all required fields
- **WHEN** The object is validated
- **THEN** Validation passes with no errors

### Requirement: CloneGroupValidation

The system SHALL validate CloneGroup according to these rules:
- similarity must be between 0 and 1

#### Scenario: ValidCloneGroupAccepted
- **GIVEN** A valid CloneGroup object with all required fields
- **WHEN** The object is validated
- **THEN** Validation passes with no errors

### Requirement: DuplicateDetectionResultValidation

The system SHALL validate DuplicateDetectionResult according to these rules:
- totalFiles must be non-negative
- totalLines must be non-negative

#### Scenario: ValidDuplicateDetectionResultAccepted
- **GIVEN** A valid DuplicateDetectionResult object with all required fields
- **WHEN** The object is validated
- **THEN** Validation passes with no errors

### Requirement: ScoredFileValidation

The system SHALL validate ScoredFile according to these rules:
- Score must be between 0 and 100
- Score breakdown must include name, path, structure, and connectivity scores

#### Scenario: ScoreFile
- **GIVEN** FileMetadata and ScoringConfig
- **WHEN** scoreFile() is called
- **THEN** ScoredFile is returned with calculated score and tags

### Requirement: Map

The system SHALL generates a comprehensive map of the repository including language breakdown, detected frameworks, directory statistics, and file clusters.

#### Scenario: SuccessfulMapping
- **GIVEN** A valid root path and options
- **WHEN** map is called
- **THEN** A complete repository map is generated

### Requirement: Writeoutput

The system SHALL writes the generated repository map to the output directory.

#### Scenario: SuccessfulWrite
- **GIVEN** A valid repository map
- **WHEN** writeOutput is called
- **THEN** The repository map is written to the output directory


## Sub-components

> `RepositoryMapper` is an orchestrator. Each sub-component below implements one logical block.

### Sub-component: Loadpackagejson

> Implements: `loadPackageJson`

Loads the package.json file from the repository root to extract project metadata.

#### Requirement: Readpackagejson

The system SHALL the function shall read the package.json file from the specified root path.

#### Scenario: Unnamed
- **GIVEN** the system is in a valid state
- **WHEN** the operation is invoked
- **THEN** the expected outcome occurs

### Sub-component: Walk

> Implements: `walk`

Walks the codebase and collects file metadata.

#### Requirement: Walkcodebase

The system SHALL the function shall walk the codebase starting from the root path and collect file metadata.

#### Scenario: Unnamed
- **GIVEN** the system is in a valid state
- **WHEN** the operation is invoked
- **THEN** the expected outcome occurs

### Sub-component: Scorefiles

Scores all files in the repository to determine their relevance and importance.

#### Requirement: Scoreallfiles

The system SHALL the function shall score each file in the provided array of file metadata.

#### Scenario: Unnamed
- **GIVEN** the system is in a valid state
- **WHEN** the operation is invoked
- **THEN** the expected outcome occurs

### Sub-component: Detectprojecttype

> Implements: `detectProjectType`

Detects the project type based on manifest files present in the repository.

#### Requirement: Detecttype

The system SHALL the function shall detect the project type based on manifest files present in the specified root path.

#### Scenario: Unnamed
- **GIVEN** the system is in a valid state
- **WHEN** the operation is invoked
- **THEN** the expected outcome occurs

### Sub-component: Calculatelanguages

> Implements: `calculateLanguages`

Calculates the programming languages used in the repository.

#### Requirement: Calculatelanguagesused

The system SHALL the function shall calculate the programming languages used in the repository based on the file extensions.

#### Scenario: Unnamed
- **GIVEN** the system is in a valid state
- **WHEN** the operation is invoked
- **THEN** the expected outcome occurs

### Sub-component: Detectframeworks

> Implements: `detectFrameworks`

Detects the frameworks used in the repository.

#### Requirement: Detectframeworksused

The system SHALL the function shall detect the frameworks used in the repository based on the file content and dependencies.

#### Scenario: Unnamed
- **GIVEN** the system is in a valid state
- **WHEN** the operation is invoked
- **THEN** the expected outcome occurs

### Sub-component: Calculatedirectorystats

Calculates statistics for each directory in the repository.

#### Requirement: Calculatedirectorystatistics

- **WHEN** the operation is invoked
- **THEN** the expected outcome occurs

Clusters files in the repository based on their domains and layers.

#### Scenario: Unnamed
- **GIVEN** the system is in a valid state
- **WHEN** the operation is invoked
- **THEN** the expected outcome occurs

### Sub-component: Getprojectname

> Implements: `getProjectName`

Retrieves the name of the project from the package.json file.

#### Requirement: Retrieveprojectname

The system SHALL the function shall retrieve the name of the project from the package.json file.

#### Scenario: Unnamed
- **GIVEN** the system is in a valid state
- **WHEN** the operation is invoked
- **THEN** the expected outcome occurs

### Requirement: Getfilegodfunctions

The system SHALL identifies all god functions (fanout >= threshold) defined in a given file.

#### Scenario: ValidFilePath
- **GIVEN** A valid file path and call graph
- **WHEN** getFileGodFunctions is called
- **THEN** Returns an array of FunctionNode objects representing god functions in the file

#### Scenario: InvalidFilePath
- **GIVEN** An invalid file path and call graph
- **WHEN** getFileGodFunctions is called
- **THEN** Returns an empty array

### Requirement: Extractsubgraph

The system SHALL extracts a depth-limited subgraph around a root node.

#### Scenario: ValidRootNode
- **GIVEN** A valid root node and call graph
- **WHEN** extractSubgraph is called
- **THEN** Returns a SubGraph object representing the subgraph around the root node

#### Scenario: InvalidRootNode
- **GIVEN** An invalid root node and call graph
- **WHEN** extractSubgraph is called
- **THEN** Returns an empty SubGraph object

### Requirement: Formatsubgraph

The system SHALL formats a single subgraph as a compact ascii block for llm prompts.

#### Scenario: ValidSubgraph
- **GIVEN** A valid SubGraph object
- **WHEN** formatSubgraph is called
- **THEN** Returns a formatted string representing the subgraph

#### Scenario: EmptySubgraph
- **GIVEN** An empty SubGraph object
- **WHEN** formatSubgraph is called
- **THEN** Returns an empty string

### Requirement: Buildgraphpromptsection

The system SHALL builds a graph-based prompt section for a large file.

#### Scenario: ValidCallGraphAndSignatures
- **GIVEN** A valid call graph, signatures, and file path
- **WHEN** buildGraphPromptSection is called
- **THEN** Returns a formatted string representing the graph-based prompt section

#### Scenario: NoGodFunctions
- **GIVEN** A call graph with no god functions and valid file path
- **WHEN** buildGraphPromptSection is called
- **THEN** Returns null

#### Scenario: NoCallGraph
- **GIVEN** No call graph and valid file path
- **WHEN** buildGraphPromptSection is called
- **THEN** Returns null

### Requirement: Inferclusterrole

The system SHALL infer a module cluster's architectural role from aggregate metrics.

#### Scenario: EntryLayer
- **GIVEN** Entry count is more than half of file count
- **WHEN** inferClusterRole is called
- **THEN** Role is 'entry_layer'

#### Scenario: Orchestrator
- **GIVEN** Both hub and entry counts are greater than zero
- **WHEN** inferClusterRole is called
- **THEN** Role is 'orchestrator'

#### Scenario: CoreUtilities
- **GIVEN** Hub count is greater than zero and entry count is zero
- **WHEN** inferClusterRole is called
- **THEN** Role is 'core_utilities'

#### Scenario: ApiLayer
- **GIVEN** Entry count is greater than zero and hub count is zero
- **WHEN** inferClusterRole is called
- **THEN** Role is 'api_layer'

#### Scenario: Internal
- **GIVEN** Neither hub nor entry counts are greater than zero
- **WHEN** inferClusterRole is called
- **THEN** Role is 'internal'

### Requirement: Buildarchitectureoverview

The system SHALL build an architectureoverview from pre-loaded dependency graph and llm context.

#### Scenario: BothArtifactsAvailable
- **GIVEN** Both depGraph and ctx are non-null
- **WHEN** buildArchitectureOverview is called
- **THEN** ArchitectureOverview is built with all data

#### Scenario: OnlyDependencyGraphAvailable
- **GIVEN** depGraph is non-null and ctx is null
- **WHEN** buildArchitectureOverview is called
- **THEN** ArchitectureOverview is built with dependency graph data

#### Scenario: OnlyLlmContextAvailable
- **GIVEN** depGraph is null and ctx is non-null
- **WHEN** buildArchitectureOverview is called
- **THEN** ArchitectureOverview is built with LLM context data

### Requirement: Renderarchitecturemarkdown

The system SHALL render an architectureoverview as a markdown document.

#### Scenario: RenderWithAllData
- **GIVEN** overview contains all data
- **WHEN** renderArchitectureMarkdown is called
- **THEN** Markdown document is rendered with all data

#### Scenario: RenderWithMissingData
- **GIVEN** overview is missing some data
- **WHEN** renderArchitectureMarkdown is called
- **THEN** Markdown document is rendered with available data

### Requirement: Build

The system SHALL builds the dependency graph from scored files.

#### Scenario: ValidFiles
- **GIVEN** An array of valid ScoredFile objects
- **WHEN** build is called
- **THEN** A complete DependencyGraphResult is returned

#### Scenario: EmptyFilesArray
- **GIVEN** An empty array of ScoredFile objects
- **WHEN** build is called
- **THEN** An empty DependencyGraphResult is returned

### Sub-component: Detectclusters

> Implements: `detectClusters`

Detects clusters in the dependency graph and suggests domain names for each cluster.

#### Requirement: Detectgraphclusters

The system SHALL the system shall detect clusters in the dependency graph and suggest domain names for each cluster.

#### Scenario: Unnamed

- **THEN** the expected outcome occurs

- **THEN** the expected outcome occurs

- **GIVEN** the system is in a valid state
- **WHEN** the operation is invoked
- **THEN** the expected outcome occurs

### Requirement: Build

The system SHALL discovers all spec.md files under specsdir, parses them, enriches with mapping, embeds, and writes to lancedb table 'specs'.

#### Scenario: SuccessfulBuild
- **GIVEN** Valid outputDir, specsDir, embedSvc, and optional mappingJsonPath
- **WHEN** build is called
- **THEN** Spec files are parsed, enriched, embedded, and written to LanceDB table 'specs'

#### Scenario: NoSpecFilesFound
- **GIVEN** No spec.md files found in specsDir
- **WHEN** build is called
- **THEN** An error is thrown indicating no spec.md files were found

### Requirement: Search

The system SHALL searches the lancedb vector index for records matching the query.

#### Scenario: SuccessfulSearch
- **GIVEN** Valid outputDir, query, and embedSvc
- **WHEN** search is called
- **THEN** Records matching the query are returned from the LanceDB vector index

### Requirement: Findspecfiles

The system SHALL finds specification files in the given directory.

#### Scenario: SpecFilesFound
- **GIVEN** Valid directory with specification files
- **WHEN** findSpecFiles is called
- **THEN** Array of specification file paths is returned

#### Scenario: SpecFilesNotFound
- **GIVEN** Directory does not exist or contains no specification files
- **WHEN** findSpecFiles is called
- **THEN** Empty array is returned

### Requirement: Walk

The system SHALL traverses the codebase starting from the root path, collecting metadata about each file.

#### Scenario: SuccessfulTraversal
- **GIVEN** Valid root path and options
- **WHEN** walk is called
- **THEN** Returns FileWalkerResult with collected file metadata

#### Scenario: TraversalCancelled
- **GIVEN** AbortSignal is triggered
- **WHEN** walk is called
- **THEN** Returns partial FileWalkerResult with collected files up to cancellation

### Requirement: Processfile

The system SHALL processes a single file, collecting metadata and determining if it should be included in the results.

#### Scenario: FileIncluded
- **GIVEN** File matches include patterns and doesn't match exclude patterns
- **WHEN** processFile is called
- **THEN** Returns FileMetadata for the file

#### Scenario: FileExcluded
- **GIVEN** File matches exclude patterns or is skipped for other reasons
- **WHEN** processFile is called
- **THEN** Returns null and increments skipped count

### Requirement: Processdirectory

The system SHALL processes a directory, checking if it should be traversed further.

#### Scenario: DirectoryIncluded
- **GIVEN** Directory doesn't match exclude patterns and isn't in SKIP_DIRECTORIES
- **WHEN** processDirectory is called
- **THEN** Returns true and increments directoriesScanned

#### Scenario: DirectoryExcluded
- **GIVEN** Directory matches exclude patterns or is in SKIP_DIRECTORIES
- **WHEN** processDirectory is called
- **THEN** Returns false and increments skipped count

### Requirement: Shouldincludefile

The system SHALL determines if a file should be included based on include and exclude patterns.

#### Scenario: FileIncluded
- **GIVEN** File matches include patterns and doesn't match exclude patterns
- **WHEN** shouldIncludeFile is called
- **THEN** Returns true

#### Scenario: FileExcluded
- **GIVEN** File matches exclude patterns or doesn't match include patterns
- **WHEN** shouldIncludeFile is called
- **THEN** Returns false

### Requirement: Shouldskipfile

The system SHALL determines if a file should be skipped based on various criteria.

#### Scenario: FileSkipped
- **GIVEN** File matches skip patterns or is in SKIP_FILENAMES or SKIP_EXTENSIONS
- **WHEN** shouldSkipFile is called
- **THEN** Returns true

#### Scenario: FileNotSkipped
- **GIVEN** File doesn't match skip patterns and isn't in SKIP_FILENAMES or SKIP_EXTENSIONS
- **WHEN** shouldSkipFile is called
- **THEN** Returns false

### Requirement: Istestfile

The system SHALL determines if a file is a test file based on patterns.

#### Scenario: TestFile
- **GIVEN** File matches test patterns
- **WHEN** isTestFile is called
- **THEN** Returns true

#### Scenario: NotTestFile
- **GIVEN** File doesn't match test patterns
- **WHEN** isTestFile is called
- **THEN** Returns false

### Requirement: Isconfigfile

The system SHALL determines if a file is a configuration file based on patterns.

#### Scenario: ConfigFile
- **GIVEN** File matches config patterns
- **WHEN** isConfigFile is called
- **THEN** Returns true

#### Scenario: NotConfigFile
- **GIVEN** File doesn't match config patterns
- **WHEN** isConfigFile is called
- **THEN** Returns false

### Requirement: Isgeneratedfile

The system SHALL determines if a file is likely generated based on patterns.

#### Scenario: GeneratedFile
- **GIVEN** File matches generated patterns
- **WHEN** isGeneratedFile is called
- **THEN** Returns true

#### Scenario: NotGeneratedFile
- **GIVEN** File doesn't match generated patterns
- **WHEN** isGeneratedFile is called
- **THEN** Returns false

### Requirement: Isentrypoint

The system SHALL determines if a file might be an entry point based on patterns and shebang.

#### Scenario: EntryPoint
- **GIVEN** File matches entry point patterns or has shebang
- **WHEN** isEntryPoint is called
- **THEN** Returns true

#### Scenario: NotEntryPoint
- **GIVEN** File doesn't match entry point patterns and doesn't have shebang
- **WHEN** isEntryPoint is called
- **THEN** Returns false

### Requirement: Hasshebang

The system SHALL determines if a file has a shebang line.

#### Scenario: HasShebang
- **GIVEN** File has shebang line
- **WHEN** hasShebang is called
- **THEN** Returns true

#### Scenario: NoShebang
- **GIVEN** File doesn't have shebang line
- **WHEN** hasShebang is called
- **THEN** Returns false

### Requirement: Countlines

The system SHALL counts the number of lines in a file.

#### Scenario: FileReadSuccessfully
- **GIVEN** File is readable and size is less than MAX_READ_SIZE
- **WHEN** countLines is called
- **THEN** Returns number of lines in the file

#### Scenario: FileTooLarge
- **GIVEN** File size is greater than MAX_READ_SIZE
- **WHEN** countLines is called
- **THEN** Returns -1

#### Scenario: FileReadError
- **GIVEN** File is not readable
- **WHEN** countLines is called
- **THEN** Returns 0

### Requirement: Analyzeforrefactoring

The system SHALL analyzes a call graph for refactoring priorities and issues.

#### Scenario: ValidCallGraphWithMappings
- **GIVEN** A valid call graph and requirement mappings
- **WHEN** analyzeForRefactoring is called
- **THEN** A RefactorReport is generated with prioritized refactoring candidates

#### Scenario: ValidCallGraphWithoutMappings
- **GIVEN** A valid call graph without requirement mappings
- **WHEN** analyzeForRefactoring is called
- **THEN** A RefactorReport is generated with prioritized refactoring candidates based on call graph metrics
only

### Requirement: Computedepths

The system SHALL computes the depth of each function node in the call graph from entry points.

#### Scenario: ValidCallGraph
- **GIVEN** A valid call graph with nodes and edges
- **WHEN** computeDepths is called
- **THEN** A map of function node IDs to their depths is returned

### Requirement: Computesccs

The system SHALL computes the strongly connected components (sccs) of the call graph using tarjan's algorithm.

#### Scenario: ValidCallGraph
- **GIVEN** A valid call graph with nodes and edges
- **WHEN** computeSCCs is called
- **THEN** A map of function node IDs to their SCC IDs is returned

### Requirement: Iscrosscuttinghub

The system SHALL determines if a high-fanin node is a cross-cutting utility sink by design.

#### Scenario: CrossCuttingUtilitySink
- **GIVEN** A function node in a utility/logging module with fanOut === 0
- **WHEN** isCrossCuttingHub is called
- **THEN** true is returned

#### Scenario: NonCrossCuttingUtilitySink
- **GIVEN** A function node not in a utility/logging module or with fanOut !== 0
- **WHEN** isCrossCuttingHub is called
- **THEN** false is returned

### Requirement: Build

The system SHALL builds or rebuilds the vector index from call graph nodes and signatures.

#### Scenario: SuccessfulBuild
- **GIVEN** Valid input parameters and existing LanceDB connection
- **WHEN** build is called
- **THEN** Vector index is built and stored in the specified output directory

#### Scenario: NoFunctionsToIndex
- **GIVEN** Empty nodes array
- **WHEN** build is called
- **THEN** Error is thrown indicating no functions to index

#### Scenario: EmbeddingCountMismatch
- **GIVEN** Mismatch between the number of texts and vectors
- **WHEN** build is called
- **THEN** Error is thrown indicating embedding count mismatch

### Requirement: Search

The system SHALL performs semantic search over the vector index.

#### Scenario: SuccessfulSearch
- **GIVEN** Valid query and existing vector index
- **WHEN** search is called
- **THEN** Search results are returned sorted by similarity

#### Scenario: FailedToEmbedQuery
- **GIVEN** Failed to embed the query
- **WHEN** search is called
- **THEN** Error is thrown indicating failed to embed query

#### Scenario: VectorIndexNotFound
- **GIVEN** Vector index does not exist in the specified output directory
- **WHEN** search is called
- **THEN** Error is thrown indicating vector index not found

### Requirement: Exists

The system SHALL checks if a vector index has been built for the specified output directory.

#### Scenario: VectorIndexExists
- **GIVEN** Vector index exists in the specified output directory
- **WHEN** exists is called
- **THEN** True is returned

#### Scenario: VectorIndexDoesNotExist
- **GIVEN** Vector index does not exist in the specified output directory
- **WHEN** exists is called
- **THEN** False is returned

### Requirement: Parsefile

The system SHALL parses a file to extract import and export information.

#### Scenario: ValidJavascriptFile
- **GIVEN** A valid JavaScript file with imports and exports
- **WHEN** parseFile is called
- **THEN** FileAnalysis with correct imports and exports is returned

#### Scenario: InvalidFilePath
- **GIVEN** An invalid file path
- **WHEN** parseFile is called
- **THEN** An error is thrown

### Requirement: Resolveimport

The system SHALL resolves an import path to an absolute path.

#### Scenario: RelativeImport
- **GIVEN** A relative import path
- **WHEN** resolveImport is called
- **THEN** The resolved absolute path is returned

#### Scenario: PackageImport
- **GIVEN** A package import path
- **WHEN** resolveImport is called
- **THEN** The resolved absolute path is returned

### Requirement: Parsejsimports

The system SHALL parses various types of import statements from javascript/typescript content.

#### Scenario: Es6NamedImports
- **GIVEN** Content with import { X, Y } from 'module'
- **WHEN** parseJSImports is called
- **THEN** Returns ImportInfo with importedNames [X, Y], isPackage true, isRelative false

#### Scenario: Es6DefaultImports
- **GIVEN** Content with import X from 'module'
- **WHEN** parseJSImports is called
- **THEN** Returns ImportInfo with hasDefault true, importedNames [X]

#### Scenario: TypeOnlyImports
- **GIVEN** Content with import type { X } from 'module'
- **WHEN** parseJSImports is called
- **THEN** Returns ImportInfo with isTypeOnly true, importedNames [X]

#### Scenario: CommonjsRequire
- **GIVEN** Content with const X = require('module')
- **WHEN** parseJSImports is called
- **THEN** Returns ImportInfo with hasDefault true, importedNames [X]

#### Scenario: DynamicImports
- **GIVEN** Content with import('module')
- **WHEN** parseJSImports is called
- **THEN** Returns ImportInfo with isDynamic true

### Requirement: Parsejsexports

The system SHALL parses various types of export statements from javascript/typescript content.

#### Scenario: DefaultExports
- **GIVEN** Content with export default X
- **WHEN** parseJSExports is called
- **THEN** Returns ExportInfo with isDefault true, name X

#### Scenario: NamedExports
- **GIVEN** Content with export { X, Y }
- **WHEN** parseJSExports is called
- **THEN** Returns ExportInfo for X and Y with isDefault false

#### Scenario: VariableExports
- **GIVEN** Content with export const X
- **WHEN** parseJSExports is called
- **THEN** Returns ExportInfo with kind 'variable', name X

#### Scenario: FunctionExports
- **GIVEN** Content with export function X()
- **WHEN** parseJSExports is called
- **THEN** Returns ExportInfo with kind 'function', name X

#### Scenario: ClassExports
- **GIVEN** Content with export class X
- **WHEN** parseJSExports is called
- **THEN** Returns ExportInfo with kind 'class', name X

#### Scenario: TypeExports
- **GIVEN** Content with export type X
- **WHEN** parseJSExports is called
- **THEN** Returns ExportInfo with isType true, name X

#### Scenario: InterfaceExports
- **GIVEN** Content with export interface X
- **WHEN** parseJSExports is called
- **THEN** Returns ExportInfo with isType true, kind 'interface', name X

#### Scenario: EnumExports
- **GIVEN** Content with export enum X
- **WHEN** parseJSExports is called
- **THEN** Returns ExportInfo with kind 'enum', name X

#### Scenario: ReExportAll
- **GIVEN** Content with export * from 'module'
- **WHEN** parseJSExports is called
- **THEN** Returns ExportInfo with isReExport true, name '*'

#### Scenario: CommonjsModule.exports
- **GIVEN** Content with module.exports = X
- **WHEN** parseJSExports is called
- **THEN** Returns ExportInfo with isDefault true, name X

#### Scenario: CommonjsExports.x
- **GIVEN** Content with exports.X = ...
- **WHEN** parseJSExports is called
- **THEN** Returns ExportInfo with name X

### Requirement: Extractsignatures

The system SHALL extracts signatures and docstrings from source files.

#### Scenario: PythonFile
- **GIVEN** A Python file with classes and functions
- **WHEN** extractSignatures is called
- **THEN** A FileSignatureMap with extracted Python signatures is returned

#### Scenario: TypescriptFile
- **GIVEN** A TypeScript file with classes, interfaces, and functions
- **WHEN** extractSignatures is called
- **THEN** A FileSignatureMap with extracted TypeScript signatures is returned

### Requirement: Detectlanguage

The system SHALL detects the programming language of a file based on its extension.

#### Scenario: PythonFile
- **GIVEN** A file with a .py extension
- **WHEN** detectLanguage is called
- **THEN** The language 'Python' is returned

#### Scenario: TypescriptFile
- **GIVEN** A file with a .ts extension
- **WHEN** detectLanguage is called
- **THEN** The language 'TypeScript' is returned

### Requirement: Generatellmcontext

The system SHALL generates llm context by analyzing repository files, extracting signatures, and building a call graph.

#### Scenario: ValidRepositoryMap
- **GIVEN** A valid repository map with files and dependencies
- **WHEN** generateLLMContext is called
- **THEN** LLM context is generated with extracted signatures and call graph

#### Scenario: EmptyRepositoryMap
- **GIVEN** An empty repository map
- **WHEN** generateLLMContext is called
- **THEN** An empty LLM context is generated

### Requirement: Istestfile

The system SHALL heuristic to detect test/spec files across languages.

#### Scenario: TestFile
- **GIVEN** A file path ending with _test.js or .spec.ts
- **WHEN** isTestFile is called
- **THEN** Returns true

#### Scenario: NonTestFile
- **GIVEN** A file path ending with .js or .ts
- **WHEN** isTestFile is called
- **THEN** Returns false

### Requirement: Detectduplicates

The system SHALL analyzes the codebase to identify duplicate code segments and groups them based on similarity.

#### Scenario: IdentifyExactDuplicates
- **GIVEN** Codebase with identical code segments
- **WHEN** detectDuplicates is called
- **THEN** DuplicateDetectionResult contains groups of identical code segments

#### Scenario: IdentifySimilarDuplicates
- **GIVEN** Codebase with similar code segments
- **WHEN** detectDuplicates is called
- **THEN** DuplicateDetectionResult contains groups of similar code segments


## Sub-components

> `DuplicateDetector` is an orchestrator. Each sub-component below implements one logical block.

### Sub-component: Byteoffsettoline

> Implements: `byteOffsetToLine`

Converts byte offsets to line numbers in a given source code string.

#### Requirement: Convertoffsettoline

The system SHALL converts a given byte offset to a line number in the source code.

#### Scenario: Unnamed
- **GIVEN** the system is in a valid state
- **WHEN** the operation is invoked
- **THEN** the expected outcome occurs

### Sub-component: Normalizetype1

> Implements: `normalizeType1`

Normalizes code segments by stripping comments and standardizing whitespace.

#### Requirement: Stripcommentsandwhitespace

The system SHALL strips comments from the code segment and standardizes whitespace.

#### Scenario: Unnamed
- **GIVEN** the system is in a valid state
- **WHEN** the operation is invoked
- **THEN** the expected outcome occurs

### Sub-component: Normalizetype2

> Implements: `normalizeType2`

Further normalizes code segments by applying additional transformations.

#### Requirement: Applyadditionaltransformations

The system SHALL applies additional transformations to the normalized code segment.

#### Scenario: Unnamed
- **GIVEN** the system is in a valid state
- **WHEN** the operation is invoked
- **THEN** the expected outcome occurs

### Sub-component: Tokenize

> Implements: `tokenize`

Tokenizes a given code segment into individual tokens.

#### Requirement: Tokenizecodesegment

The system SHALL tokenizes the given code segment into individual tokens.

#### Scenario: Unnamed
- **GIVEN** the system is in a valid state
- **WHEN** the operation is invoked
- **THEN** the expected outcome occurs

### Sub-component: Push

> Implements: `push`

Pushes a new element onto the end of an array.

#### Requirement: Pushelement

The system SHALL pushes a new element onto the end of the array.

#### Scenario: Unnamed
- **GIVEN** the system is in a valid state
- **WHEN** the operation is invoked
- **THEN** the expected outcome occurs

### Sub-component: Sha16

> Implements: `sha16`

Computes the SHA-1 hash of a given input and returns the first 16 characters.

#### Requirement: Computesha16

The system SHALL computes the sha-1 hash of the input and returns the first 16 characters.

#### Scenario: Unnamed
- **GIVEN** the system is in a valid state
- **WHEN** the operation is invoked
- **THEN** the expected outcome occurs

### Sub-component: Getshingles

> Implements: `getShingles`

Generates shingles (contiguous sequences of tokens) from a given array of tokens.

#### Requirement: Generateshingles

The system SHALL generates shingles from the given array of tokens.

#### Scenario: Unnamed
- **GIVEN** the system is in a valid state
- **WHEN** the operation is invoked
- **THEN** the expected outcome occurs

### Sub-component: Jaccard

> Implements: `jaccard`

Computes the Jaccard similarity between two sets of shingles.

#### Requirement: Computejaccardsimilarity

The system SHALL computes the jaccard similarity between two sets of shingles.

#### Scenario: Unnamed
- **GIVEN** the system is in a valid state
- **WHEN** the operation is invoked
- **THEN** the expected outcome occurs

### Requirement: Calculatenamescore

The system SHALL calculates the name-based score for a file based on its name and custom configuration.

#### Scenario: HighValueName
- **GIVEN** File name contains 'model'
- **WHEN** calculateNameScore is called
- **THEN** Score is 25

#### Scenario: NegativeName
- **GIVEN** File name contains 'test'
- **WHEN** calculateNameScore is called
- **THEN** Score is -10

### Requirement: Calculatepathscore

The system SHALL calculates the path-based score for a file based on its path, depth, and custom configuration.

#### Scenario: HighValuePath
- **GIVEN** File path starts with 'src/'
- **WHEN** calculatePathScore is called
- **THEN** Score is 10

#### Scenario: DeeplyNestedFile
- **GIVEN** File depth is 6
- **WHEN** calculatePathScore is called
- **THEN** Score is reduced by 10

### Requirement: Calculatestructurescore

The system SHALL calculates the structure-based score for a file based on its content.

#### Scenario: FileWithClassDefinitions
- **GIVEN** File content contains class definitions
- **WHEN** calculateStructureScore is called
- **THEN** Score is increased by 10

#### Scenario: LargeFile
- **GIVEN** File has more than 1000 lines
- **WHEN** calculateStructureScore is called
- **THEN** Score is reduced by 5

### Requirement: Buildfilerelationships

The system SHALL builds file relationships from import analysis.

#### Scenario: FilesWithImports
- **GIVEN** Files have import statements
- **WHEN** buildFileRelationships is called
- **THEN** Relationships map is built with import information

### Requirement: Calculateconnectivityscore

The system SHALL calculates the connectivity score for a file based on its import relationships.

#### Scenario: FileImportedByManyFiles
- **GIVEN** File is imported by 5 other files
- **WHEN** calculateConnectivityScore is called
- **THEN** Score is 20

#### Scenario: OrphanFile
- **GIVEN** File has no imports or imports by other files
- **WHEN** calculateConnectivityScore is called
- **THEN** Score is reduced by 10

### Requirement: Getfunctionskeleton

The system SHALL returns a noise-stripped skeleton of a source file.

#### Scenario: ValidFile
- **GIVEN** A valid source file
- **WHEN** getFunctionSkeleton is called with the file path
- **THEN** Returns the skeleton of the source file with metadata

#### Scenario: InvalidFile
- **GIVEN** An invalid file path
- **WHEN** getFunctionSkeleton is called with the file path
- **THEN** Returns an error indicating the file was not found

### Requirement: Getskeletoncontent

The system SHALL strips implementation noise from source code while preserving the logical skeleton.

#### Scenario: ValidSourceCode
- **GIVEN** Source code with logs and comments
- **WHEN** getSkeletonContent is called
- **THEN** Returns skeleton content without logs and comments

### Requirement: Detectlanguage

The system SHALL detects the programming language of a file based on its extension.

#### Scenario: ValidFilePath
- **GIVEN** File path with a known extension
- **WHEN** detectLanguage is called
- **THEN** Returns the corresponding programming language

### Requirement: Isskeletonworthincluding

The system SHALL determines if the skeleton content is worth including based on the reduction ratio.

#### Scenario: ValidInput
- **GIVEN** Original and skeleton content
- **WHEN** isSkeletonWorthIncluding is called
- **THEN** Returns true if the skeleton is at least 20% smaller than the original
